  67. /**

  76.  
  77. /** 
  78.  * Return the current TCPDF producer. 
  79.  * @return TCPDF producer string 
  80.  * @since 6.0.000 (2013-03-16) 
  81.  * @public static 
  82.  */ 
  83. public static function getTCPDFProducer() { 
  84.     return "\x54\x43\x50\x44\x46\x20".self::getTCPDFVersion()."\x20\x28\x68\x74\x74\x70\x3a\x2f\x2f\x77\x77\x77\x2e\x74\x63\x70\x64\x66\x2e\x6f\x72\x67\x29"; 
  85. }

  87. /** 
  88.  * Sets the current active configuration setting of magic_quotes_runtime (if the set_magic_quotes_runtime function exist) 
  89.  * @param $mqr (boolean) FALSE for off, TRUE for on. 
  90.  * @since 4.6.025 (2009-08-17) 
  91.  * @public static 
  92.  */ 
  93. public static function set_mqr($mqr) { 
  94.     if (!defined('PHP_VERSION_ID')) { 
  95.         $version = PHP_VERSION; 
  96.         define('PHP_VERSION_ID', (($version[0] * 10000) + ($version[2] * 100) + $version[4])); 
  97.     } 
  98.     if (PHP_VERSION_ID < 50300) { 
  99.         @set_magic_quotes_runtime($mqr); 
  100.     } 
  101. } 
  102.  
  103. /** 
  104.  * Gets the current active configuration setting of magic_quotes_runtime (if the get_magic_quotes_runtime function exist) 
  105.  * @return Returns 0 if magic quotes runtime is off or get_magic_quotes_runtime doesn't exist, 1 otherwise. 
  106.  * @since 4.6.025 (2009-08-17) 
  107.  * @public static 
  108.  */ 
  109. public static function get_mqr() { 
  110.     if (!defined('PHP_VERSION_ID')) { 
  111.         $version = PHP_VERSION; 
  112.         define('PHP_VERSION_ID', (($version[0] * 10000) + ($version[2] * 100) + $version[4])); 
  113.     } 
  114.     if (PHP_VERSION_ID < 50300) { 
  115.         return @get_magic_quotes_runtime(); 
  116.     } 
  117.     return 0; 
  118. }

  433.  */ 
  434. public static function getPageSizeFromFormat($format) { 
  435.     // Paper cordinates are calculated in this way: (inches * 72) where (1 inch = 25.4 mm) 
  436.     switch (strtoupper($format)) {

  438.         case 'A0' : {$pf = array( 2383.937, 3370.394); break;}

  788. /** 
  789.  * Set page boundaries. 
  790.  * @param $page (int) page number 
  791.  * @param $type (string) valid values are: <ul><li>'MediaBox' : the boundaries of the physical medium on which the page shall be displayed or printed;</li><li>'CropBox' : the visible region of default user space;</li><li>'BleedBox' : the region to which the contents of the page shall be clipped when output in a production environment;</li><li>'TrimBox' : the intended dimensions of the finished page after trimming;</li><li>'ArtBox' : the page's meaningful content (including potential white space).</li></ul> 
  792.  * @param $llx (float) lower-left x coordinate in user units. 
  793.  * @param $lly (float) lower-left y coordinate in user units. 
  794.  * @param $urx (float) upper-right x coordinate in user units. 
  795.  * @param $ury (float) upper-right y coordinate in user units. 
  796.  * @param $points (boolean) If true uses user units as unit of measure, otherwise uses PDF points. 
  797.  * @param $k (float) Scale factor (number of points in user unit). 
  798.  * @param $pagedim (array) Array of page dimensions. 
  799.  * @return pagedim array of page dimensions. 
  800.  * @since 5.0.010 (2010-05-17) 
  801.  * @public static 
  802.  */ 
  803. public static function setPageBoxes($page, $type, $llx, $lly, $urx, $ury, $points=false, $k, $pagedim=array()) { 
  804.     if (!isset($pagedim[$page])) { 
  805.         // initialize array 
  806.         $pagedim[$page] = array(); 
  807.     } 
  808.     if (!in_array($type, self::$pageboxes)) { 
  809.         return; 
  810.     } 
  811.     if ($points) { 
  812.         $k = 1; 
  813.     } 
  814.     $pagedim[$page][$type]['llx'] = ($llx * $k); 
  815.     $pagedim[$page][$type]['lly'] = ($lly * $k); 
  816.     $pagedim[$page][$type]['urx'] = ($urx * $k); 
  817.     $pagedim[$page][$type]['ury'] = ($ury * $k); 
  818.     return $pagedim; 
  819. } 
  820.  
  821. /** 
  822.  * Swap X and Y coordinates of page boxes (change page boxes orientation). 
  823.  * @param $page (int) page number 
  824.  * @param $pagedim (array) Array of page dimensions. 
  825.  * @return pagedim array of page dimensions. 
  826.  * @since 5.0.010 (2010-05-17) 
  827.  * @public static 
  828.  */ 
  829. public static function swapPageBoxCoordinates($page, $pagedim) { 
  830.     foreach (self::$pageboxes as $type) { 
  831.         // swap X and Y coordinates 
  832.         if (isset($pagedim[$page][$type])) { 
  833.             $tmp = $pagedim[$page][$type]['llx']; 
  834.             $pagedim[$page][$type]['llx'] = $pagedim[$page][$type]['lly']; 
  835.             $pagedim[$page][$type]['lly'] = $tmp; 
  836.             $tmp = $pagedim[$page][$type]['urx']; 
  837.             $pagedim[$page][$type]['urx'] = $pagedim[$page][$type]['ury']; 
  838.             $pagedim[$page][$type]['ury'] = $tmp; 
  839.         } 
  840.     } 
  841.     return $pagedim; 
  842. } 
  843.  
  844. /** 
  845.  * Get the canonical page layout mode. 
  846.  * @param $layout (string) The page layout. Possible values are:<ul><li>SinglePage Display one page at a time</li><li>OneColumn Display the pages in one column</li><li>TwoColumnLeft Display the pages in two columns, with odd-numbered pages on the left</li><li>TwoColumnRight Display the pages in two columns, with odd-numbered pages on the right</li><li>TwoPageLeft (PDF 1.5) Display the pages two at a time, with odd-numbered pages on the left</li><li>TwoPageRight (PDF 1.5) Display the pages two at a time, with odd-numbered pages on the right</li></ul> 
  847.  * @return (string) Canonical page layout name. 
  848.  * @public static 
  849.  */ 
  850. public static function getPageLayoutMode($layout='SinglePage') { 
  851.     switch ($layout) { 
  852.         case 'default': 
  853.         case 'single': 
  854.         case 'SinglePage': { 
  855.             $layout_mode = 'SinglePage'; 
  856.             break; 
  857.         } 
  858.         case 'continuous': 
  859.         case 'OneColumn': { 
  860.             $layout_mode = 'OneColumn'; 
  861.             break; 
  862.         } 
  863.         case 'two': 
  864.         case 'TwoColumnLeft': { 
  865.             $layout_mode = 'TwoColumnLeft'; 
  866.             break; 
  867.         } 
  868.         case 'TwoColumnRight': { 
  869.             $layout_mode = 'TwoColumnRight'; 
  870.             break; 
  871.         } 
  872.         case 'TwoPageLeft': { 
  873.             $layout_mode = 'TwoPageLeft'; 
  874.             break; 
  875.         } 
  876.         case 'TwoPageRight': { 
  877.             $layout_mode = 'TwoPageRight'; 
  878.             break; 
  879.         } 
  880.         default: { 
  881.             $layout_mode = 'SinglePage'; 
  882.         } 
  883.     } 
  884.     return $layout_mode; 
  885. } 
  886.  
  887. /** 
  888.  * Get the canonical page layout mode. 
  889.  * @param $mode (string) A name object specifying how the document should be displayed when opened:<ul><li>UseNone Neither document outline nor thumbnail images visible</li><li>UseOutlines Document outline visible</li><li>UseThumbs Thumbnail images visible</li><li>FullScreen Full-screen mode, with no menu bar, window controls, or any other window visible</li><li>UseOC (PDF 1.5) Optional content group panel visible</li><li>UseAttachments (PDF 1.6) Attachments panel visible</li></ul> 
  890.  * @return (string) Canonical page mode name. 
  891.  * @public static 
  892.  */ 
  893. public static function getPageMode($mode='UseNone') { 
  894.     switch ($mode) { 
  895.         case 'UseNone': { 
  896.             $page_mode = 'UseNone'; 
  897.             break; 
  898.         } 
  899.         case 'UseOutlines': { 
  900.             $page_mode = 'UseOutlines'; 
  901.             break; 
  902.         } 
  903.         case 'UseThumbs': { 
  904.             $page_mode = 'UseThumbs'; 
  905.             break; 
  906.         } 
  907.         case 'FullScreen': { 
  908.             $page_mode = 'FullScreen'; 
  909.             break; 
  910.         } 
  911.         case 'UseOC': { 
  912.             $page_mode = 'UseOC'; 
  913.             break; 
  914.         } 
  915.         case '': { 
  916.             $page_mode = 'UseAttachments'; 
  917.             break; 
  918.         } 
  919.         default: { 
  920.             $page_mode = 'UseNone'; 
  921.         } 
  922.     } 
  923.     return $page_mode; 
  924. } 
  925.  
  926. /** 
  927.  * Check if the URL exist. 
  928.  * @param $url (string) URL to check. 
  929.  * @return Boolean true if the URl exist, false otherwise. 
  930.  * @since 5.9.204 (2013-01-28) 
  931.  * @public static 
  932.  */ 
  933. public static function isValidURL($url) { 
  934.     $headers = @get_headers($url); 
  935.     return (strpos($headers[0], '200') !== false); 
  936. } 
  937.  
  938. /** 
  939.  * Removes SHY characters from text. 
  940.  * Unicode Data:<ul> 
  941.  * <li>Name : SOFT HYPHEN, commonly abbreviated as SHY</li> 
  942.  * <li>HTML Entity (decimal): "&#173;"</li> 
  943.  * <li>HTML Entity (hex): "&#xad;"</li> 
  944.  * <li>HTML Entity (named): "&shy;"</li> 
  945.  * <li>How to type in Microsoft Windows: [Alt +00AD] or [Alt 0173]</li> 
  946.  * <li>UTF-8 (hex): 0xC2 0xAD (c2ad)</li> 
  947.  * <li>UTF-8 character: chr(194).chr(173)</li> 
  948.  * </ul> 
  949.  * @param $txt (string) input string 
  950.  * @param $unicode (boolean) True if we are in unicode mode, false otherwise. 
  951.  * @return string without SHY characters. 
  952.  * @since (4.5.019) 2009-02-28 
  953.  * @public static 
  954.  */ 
  955. public static function removeSHY($txt='', $unicode=true) { 
  956.     $txt = preg_replace('/([\\xc2]{1}[\\xad]{1})/', '', $txt); 
  957.     if (!$unicode) { 
  958.         $txt = preg_replace('/([\\xad]{1})/', '', $txt); 
  959.     } 
  960.     return $txt; 
  961. } 
  962.  
  963.  
  964. /** 
  965.  * Get the border mode accounting for multicell position (opens bottom side of multicell crossing pages) 
  966.  * @param $brd (mixed) Indicates if borders must be drawn around the cell block. The value can be a number:<ul><li>0: no border (default)</li><li>1: frame</li></ul>or a string containing some or all of the following characters (in any order):<ul><li>L: left</li><li>T: top</li><li>R: right</li><li>B: bottom</li></ul> or an array of line styles for each border group: array('LTRB' => array('width' => 2, 'cap' => 'butt', 'join' => 'miter', 'dash' => 0, 'color' => array(0, 0, 0))) 
  967.  * @param $position (string) multicell position: 'start', 'middle', 'end' 
  968.  * @param $opencell (boolean) True when the cell is left open at the page bottom, false otherwise. 
  969.  * @return border mode array 
  970.  * @since 4.3.002 (2008-12-09) 
  971.  * @public static 
  972.  */ 
  973. public static function getBorderMode($brd, $position='start', $opencell=true) { 
  974.     if ((!$opencell) OR empty($brd)) { 
  975.         return $brd; 
  976.     } 
  977.     if ($brd == 1) { 
  978.         $brd = 'LTRB'; 
  979.     } 
  980.     if (is_string($brd)) { 
  981.         // convert string to array 
  982.         $slen = strlen($brd); 
  983.         $newbrd = array(); 
  984.         for ($i = 0; $i < $slen; ++$i) { 
  985.             $newbrd[$brd[$i]] = array('cap' => 'square', 'join' => 'miter'); 
  986.         } 
  987.         $brd = $newbrd; 
  988.     } 
  989.     foreach ($brd as $border => $style) { 
  990.         switch ($position) { 
  991.             case 'start': { 
  992.                 if (strpos($border, 'B') !== false) { 
  993.                     // remove bottom line 
  994.                     $newkey = str_replace('B', '', $border); 
  995.                     if (strlen($newkey) > 0) { 
  996.                         $brd[$newkey] = $style; 
  997.                     } 
  998.                     unset($brd[$border]); 
  999.                 } 
  1000.                 break; 
  1001.             } 
  1002.             case 'middle': { 
  1003.                 if (strpos($border, 'B') !== false) { 
  1004.                     // remove bottom line 
  1005.                     $newkey = str_replace('B', '', $border); 
  1006.                     if (strlen($newkey) > 0) { 
  1007.                         $brd[$newkey] = $style; 
  1008.                     } 
  1009.                     unset($brd[$border]); 
  1010.                     $border = $newkey; 
  1011.                 } 
  1012.                 if (strpos($border, 'T') !== false) { 
  1013.                     // remove bottom line 
  1014.                     $newkey = str_replace('T', '', $border); 
  1015.                     if (strlen($newkey) > 0) { 
  1016.                         $brd[$newkey] = $style; 
  1017.                     } 
  1018.                     unset($brd[$border]); 
  1019.                 } 
  1020.                 break; 
  1021.             } 
  1022.             case 'end': { 
  1023.                 if (strpos($border, 'T') !== false) { 
  1024.                     // remove bottom line 
  1025.                     $newkey = str_replace('T', '', $border); 
  1026.                     if (strlen($newkey) > 0) { 
  1027.                         $brd[$newkey] = $style; 
  1028.                     } 
  1029.                     unset($brd[$border]); 
  1030.                 } 
  1031.                 break; 
  1032.             } 
  1033.         } 
  1034.     } 
  1035.     return $brd; 
  1036. } 
  1037.

  1047. }

  1060. /**

  1065.  */ 
  1066. public static function _escape($s) {

  1068.     return strtr($s, array(')' => '\\)', '(' => '\\(', '\\' => '\\\\', chr(13) => '\r'));

  1071. /**

  1078. public static function _escapeXML($str) {

  1084. /**

  1114. /** 
  1115.  * Replace page number aliases with number. 
  1116.  * @param $page (string) Page content. 
  1117.  * @param $replace (array) Array of replacements (array keys are replacement strings, values are alias arrays). 
  1118.  * @param $diff (int) If passed, this will be set to the total char number difference between alias and replacements. 
  1119.  * @return replaced page content and updated $diff parameter as array. 
  1120.  * @public static 
  1121.  */ 
  1122. public static function replacePageNumAliases($page, $replace, $diff=0) { 
  1123.     foreach ($replace as $rep) { 
  1124.         foreach ($rep[3] as $a) { 
  1125.             if (strpos($page, $a) !== false) { 
  1126.                 $page = str_replace($a, $rep[0], $page); 
  1127.                 $diff += ($rep[2] - $rep[1]); 
  1128.             } 
  1129.         } 
  1130.     } 
  1131.     return array($page, $diff); 
  1132. }

  1134. /**

  1160. /**

  1169. public static function _getULONG($str, $offset) {

  1202. /** 
  1203.  * Get FWORD from string (Big Endian 16-bit signed integer). 
  1204.  * @param $str (string) String from where to extract value. 
  1205.  * @param $offset (int) Point from where to read the data. 
  1206.  * @return int 16 bit value 
  1207.  * @author Nicola Asuni 
  1208.  * @since 5.9.123 (2011-09-30) 
  1209.  * @public static 
  1210.  */ 
  1211. public static function _getFWORD($str, $offset) { 
  1212.     $v = self::_getUSHORT($str, $offset); 
  1213.     if ($v > 0x7fff) { 
  1214.         $v -= 0x10000; 
  1215.     } 
  1216.     return $v; 
  1217. }

  1233. /** 
  1234.  * Get FIXED from string (32-bit signed fixed-point number (16.16). 
  1235.  * @param $str (string) string from where to extract value 
  1236.  * @param $offset (int) point from where to read the data 
  1237.  * @return int 16 bit value

  1242. public static function _getFIXED($str, $offset) { 
  1243.     // mantissa 
  1244.     $m = self::_getFWORD($str, $offset); 
  1245.     // fraction 
  1246.     $f = self::_getUSHORT($str, ($offset + 2)); 
  1247.     $v = floatval(''.$m.'.'.$f.''); 
  1248.     return $v; 
  1249. }

  1264. /** 
  1265.  * Binary-safe and URL-safe file read. 
  1266.  * Reads up to length bytes from the file pointer referenced by handle. Reading stops as soon as one of the following conditions is met: length bytes have been read; EOF (end of file) is reached. 
  1267.  * @param $handle (resource) 
  1268.  * @param $length (int) 
  1269.  * @return Returns the read string or FALSE in case of error. 
  1270.  * @author Nicola Asuni 
  1271.  * @since 4.5.027 (2009-03-16) 
  1272.  * @public static 
  1273.  */ 
  1274. public static function rfread($handle, $length) { 
  1275.     $data = fread($handle, $length); 
  1276.     if ($data === false) { 
  1277.         return false; 
  1278.     } 
  1279.     $rest = ($length - strlen($data)); 
  1280.     if ($rest > 0) { 
  1281.         $data .= self::rfread($handle, $rest); 
  1282.     } 
  1283.     return $data; 
  1284. }
