  926. /** 
  927.  * Check if the URL exist. 
  928.  * @param $url (string) URL to check. 
  929.  * @return Boolean true if the URl exist, false otherwise. 
  930.  * @since 5.9.204 (2013-01-28) 
  931.  * @public static 
  932.  */ 
  933. public static function isValidURL($url) { 
  934.     $headers = @get_headers($url); 
  935.     return (strpos($headers[0], '200') !== false); 
  936. } 
  937.  
  938. /** 
  939.  * Removes SHY characters from text. 
  940.  * Unicode Data:<ul> 
  941.  * <li>Name : SOFT HYPHEN, commonly abbreviated as SHY</li> 
  942.  * <li>HTML Entity (decimal): "&#173;"</li> 
  943.  * <li>HTML Entity (hex): "&#xad;"</li> 
  944.  * <li>HTML Entity (named): "&shy;"</li> 
  945.  * <li>How to type in Microsoft Windows: [Alt +00AD] or [Alt 0173]</li> 
  946.  * <li>UTF-8 (hex): 0xC2 0xAD (c2ad)</li> 
  947.  * <li>UTF-8 character: chr(194).chr(173)</li> 
  948.  * </ul> 
  949.  * @param $txt (string) input string 
  950.  * @param $unicode (boolean) True if we are in unicode mode, false otherwise. 
  951.  * @return string without SHY characters. 
  952.  * @since (4.5.019) 2009-02-28 
  953.  * @public static 
  954.  */ 
  955. public static function removeSHY($txt='', $unicode=true) { 
  956.     $txt = preg_replace('/([\\xc2]{1}[\\xad]{1})/', '', $txt); 
  957.     if (!$unicode) { 
  958.         $txt = preg_replace('/([\\xad]{1})/', '', $txt); 
  959.     } 
  960.     return $txt; 
  961. } 
  962.  
  963.  
  964. /** 
  965.  * Get the border mode accounting for multicell position (opens bottom side of multicell crossing pages) 
  966.  * @param $brd (mixed) Indicates if borders must be drawn around the cell block. The value can be a number:<ul><li>0: no border (default)</li><li>1: frame</li></ul>or a string containing some or all of the following characters (in any order):<ul><li>L: left</li><li>T: top</li><li>R: right</li><li>B: bottom</li></ul> or an array of line styles for each border group: array('LTRB' => array('width' => 2, 'cap' => 'butt', 'join' => 'miter', 'dash' => 0, 'color' => array(0, 0, 0))) 
  967.  * @param $position (string) multicell position: 'start', 'middle', 'end' 
  968.  * @param $opencell (boolean) True when the cell is left open at the page bottom, false otherwise. 
  969.  * @return border mode array 
  970.  * @since 4.3.002 (2008-12-09) 
  971.  * @public static 
  972.  */ 
  973. public static function getBorderMode($brd, $position='start', $opencell=true) { 
  974.     if ((!$opencell) OR empty($brd)) { 
  975.         return $brd; 
  976.     } 
  977.     if ($brd == 1) { 
  978.         $brd = 'LTRB'; 
  979.     } 
  980.     if (is_string($brd)) { 
  981.         // convert string to array 
  982.         $slen = strlen($brd); 
  983.         $newbrd = array(); 
  984.         for ($i = 0; $i < $slen; ++$i) { 
  985.             $newbrd[$brd[$i]] = array('cap' => 'square', 'join' => 'miter'); 
  986.         } 
  987.         $brd = $newbrd; 
  988.     } 
  989.     foreach ($brd as $border => $style) { 
  990.         switch ($position) { 
  991.             case 'start': { 
  992.                 if (strpos($border, 'B') !== false) { 
  993.                     // remove bottom line 
  994.                     $newkey = str_replace('B', '', $border); 
  995.                     if (strlen($newkey) > 0) { 
  996.                         $brd[$newkey] = $style; 
  997.                     } 
  998.                     unset($brd[$border]); 
  999.                 } 
  1000.                 break; 
  1001.             } 
  1002.             case 'middle': { 
  1003.                 if (strpos($border, 'B') !== false) { 
  1004.                     // remove bottom line 
  1005.                     $newkey = str_replace('B', '', $border); 
  1006.                     if (strlen($newkey) > 0) { 
  1007.                         $brd[$newkey] = $style; 
  1008.                     } 
  1009.                     unset($brd[$border]); 
  1010.                     $border = $newkey; 
  1011.                 } 
  1012.                 if (strpos($border, 'T') !== false) { 
  1013.                     // remove bottom line 
  1014.                     $newkey = str_replace('T', '', $border); 
  1015.                     if (strlen($newkey) > 0) { 
  1016.                         $brd[$newkey] = $style; 
  1017.                     } 
  1018.                     unset($brd[$border]); 
  1019.                 } 
  1020.                 break; 
  1021.             } 
  1022.             case 'end': { 
  1023.                 if (strpos($border, 'T') !== false) { 
  1024.                     // remove bottom line 
  1025.                     $newkey = str_replace('T', '', $border); 
  1026.                     if (strlen($newkey) > 0) { 
  1027.                         $brd[$newkey] = $style; 
  1028.                     } 
  1029.                     unset($brd[$border]); 
  1030.                 } 
  1031.                 break; 
  1032.             } 
  1033.         } 
  1034.     } 
  1035.     return $brd; 
  1036. } 
  1037.  
  1038. /** 
  1039.  * Determine whether a string is empty. 
  1040.  * @param $str (string) string to be checked 
  1041.  * @return boolean true if string is empty 
  1042.  * @since 4.5.044 (2009-04-16) 
  1043.  * @public static 
  1044.  */ 
  1045. public static function empty_string($str) { 
  1046.     return (is_null($str) OR (is_string($str) AND (strlen($str) == 0))); 
  1047. } 
  1048.  
  1049. /** 
  1050.  * Returns a temporary filename for caching object on filesystem. 
  1051.  * @param $type (string) Type of file (name of the subdir on the tcpdf cache folder). 
  1052.  * @return string filename. 
  1053.  * @since 4.5.000 (2008-12-31) 
  1054.  * @public static 
  1055.  */ 
  1056. public static function getObjFilename($type='tmp') { 
  1057.     return tempnam(K_PATH_CACHE, '__tcpdf_'.$type.'_'.md5(getmypid().uniqid('', true).rand().microtime(true)).'_'); 
  1058. } 
  1059.  
  1060. /** 
  1061.  * Add "\" before "\", "(" and ")" 
  1062.  * @param $s (string) string to escape. 
  1063.  * @return string escaped string. 
  1064.  * @public static 
  1065.  */ 
  1066. public static function _escape($s) { 
  1067.     // the chr(13) substitution fixes the Bugs item #1421290. 
  1068.     return strtr($s, array(')' => '\\)', '(' => '\\(', '\\' => '\\\\', chr(13) => '\r')); 
  1069. } 
  1070.  
  1071. /** 
  1072. * Escape some special characters (< > &) for XML output. 
  1073. * @param $str (string) Input string to convert. 
  1074. * @return converted string 
  1075. * @since 5.9.121 (2011-09-28) 
  1076.  * @public static 
  1077.  */ 
  1078. public static function _escapeXML($str) { 
  1079.     $replaceTable = array("\0" => '', '&' => '&', '<' => '<', '>' => '>'); 
  1080.     $str = strtr($str, $replaceTable); 
  1081.     return $str; 
  1082. }

  1084. /** 
  1085.  * Creates a copy of a class object 
  1086.  * @param $object (object) class object to be cloned 
  1087.  * @return cloned object 
  1088.  * @since 4.5.029 (2009-03-19) 
  1089.  * @public static 
  1090.  */ 
  1091. public static function objclone($object) { 
  1092.     if (($object instanceof Imagick) AND (version_compare(phpversion('imagick'), '3.0.1') !== 1)) { 
  1093.         // on the versions after 3.0.1 the clone() method was deprecated in favour of clone keyword 
  1094.         return @$object->clone(); 
  1095.     } 
  1096.     return @clone($object); 
  1097. }

  1099. /** 
  1100.  * Ouput input data and compress it if possible. 
  1101.  * @param $data (string) Data to output. 
  1102.  * @param $length (int) Data length in bytes. 
  1103.  * @since 5.9.086 
  1104.  * @public static 
  1105.  */ 
  1106. public static function sendOutputData($data, $length) { 
  1107.     if (!isset($_SERVER['HTTP_ACCEPT_ENCODING']) OR empty($_SERVER['HTTP_ACCEPT_ENCODING'])) { 
  1108.         // the content length may vary if the server is using compression 
  1109.         header('Content-Length: '.$length); 
  1110.     } 
  1111.     echo $data; 
  1112. } 
  1113.  
  1114. /** 
  1115.  * Replace page number aliases with number. 
  1116.  * @param $page (string) Page content. 
  1117.  * @param $replace (array) Array of replacements (array keys are replacement strings, values are alias arrays). 
  1118.  * @param $diff (int) If passed, this will be set to the total char number difference between alias and replacements. 
  1119.  * @return replaced page content and updated $diff parameter as array. 
  1120.  * @public static 
  1121.  */ 
  1122. public static function replacePageNumAliases($page, $replace, $diff=0) { 
  1123.     foreach ($replace as $rep) { 
  1124.         foreach ($rep[3] as $a) { 
  1125.             if (strpos($page, $a) !== false) { 
  1126.                 $page = str_replace($a, $rep[0], $page); 
  1127.                 $diff += ($rep[2] - $rep[1]); 
  1128.             } 
  1129.         } 
  1130.     } 
  1131.     return array($page, $diff); 
  1132. } 
  1133.  
  1134. /** 
  1135.  * Returns timestamp in seconds from formatted date-time. 
  1136.  * @param $date (string) Formatted date-time. 
  1137.  * @return int seconds. 
  1138.  * @since 5.9.152 (2012-03-23) 
  1139.  * @public static 
  1140.  */ 
  1141. public static function getTimestamp($date) { 
  1142.     if (($date[0] == 'D') AND ($date[1] == ':')) { 
  1143.         // remove date prefix if present 
  1144.         $date = substr($date, 2); 
  1145.     } 
  1146.     return strtotime($date); 
  1147. } 
  1148.  
  1149. /** 
  1150.  * Returns a formatted date-time. 
  1151.  * @param $time (int) Time in seconds. 
  1152.  * @return string escaped date string. 
  1153.  * @since 5.9.152 (2012-03-23) 
  1154.  * @public static 
  1155.  */ 
  1156. public static function getFormattedDate($time) { 
  1157.     return substr_replace(date('YmdHisO', intval($time)), '\'', (0 - 2), 0).'\''; 
  1158. } 
  1159.  
  1160. /** 
  1161.  * Get ULONG from string (Big Endian 32-bit unsigned integer). 
  1162.  * @param $str (string) string from where to extract value 
  1163.  * @param $offset (int) point from where to read the data 
  1164.  * @return int 32 bit value 
  1165.  * @author Nicola Asuni 
  1166.  * @since 5.2.000 (2010-06-02) 
  1167.  * @public static 
  1168.  */ 
  1169. public static function _getULONG($str, $offset) { 
  1170.     $v = unpack('Ni', substr($str, $offset, 4)); 
  1171.     return $v['i']; 
  1172. } 
  1173.  
  1174. /** 
  1175.  * Get USHORT from string (Big Endian 16-bit unsigned integer). 
  1176.  * @param $str (string) string from where to extract value 
  1177.  * @param $offset (int) point from where to read the data 
  1178.  * @return int 16 bit value 
  1179.  * @author Nicola Asuni 
  1180.  * @since 5.2.000 (2010-06-02) 
  1181.  * @public static 
  1182.  */ 
  1183. public static function _getUSHORT($str, $offset) { 
  1184.     $v = unpack('ni', substr($str, $offset, 2)); 
  1185.     return $v['i']; 
  1186. } 
  1187.  
  1188. /** 
  1189.  * Get SHORT from string (Big Endian 16-bit signed integer). 
  1190.  * @param $str (string) String from where to extract value. 
  1191.  * @param $offset (int) Point from where to read the data. 
  1192.  * @return int 16 bit value 
  1193.  * @author Nicola Asuni 
  1194.  * @since 5.2.000 (2010-06-02) 
  1195.  * @public static 
  1196.  */ 
  1197. public static function _getSHORT($str, $offset) { 
  1198.     $v = unpack('si', substr($str, $offset, 2)); 
  1199.     return $v['i']; 
  1200. } 
  1201.  
  1202. /** 
  1203.  * Get FWORD from string (Big Endian 16-bit signed integer). 
  1204.  * @param $str (string) String from where to extract value. 
  1205.  * @param $offset (int) Point from where to read the data. 
  1206.  * @return int 16 bit value 
  1207.  * @author Nicola Asuni 
  1208.  * @since 5.9.123 (2011-09-30) 
  1209.  * @public static 
  1210.  */ 
  1211. public static function _getFWORD($str, $offset) { 
  1212.     $v = self::_getUSHORT($str, $offset); 
  1213.     if ($v > 0x7fff) { 
  1214.         $v -= 0x10000; 
  1215.     } 
  1216.     return $v; 
  1217. } 
  1218.  
  1219. /** 
  1220.  * Get UFWORD from string (Big Endian 16-bit unsigned integer). 
  1221.  * @param $str (string) string from where to extract value 
  1222.  * @param $offset (int) point from where to read the data 
  1223.  * @return int 16 bit value 
  1224.  * @author Nicola Asuni 
  1225.  * @since 5.9.123 (2011-09-30) 
  1226.  * @public static 
  1227.  */ 
  1228. public static function _getUFWORD($str, $offset) { 
  1229.     $v = self::_getUSHORT($str, $offset); 
  1230.     return $v; 
  1231. } 
  1232.  
  1233. /** 
  1234.  * Get FIXED from string (32-bit signed fixed-point number (16.16). 
  1235.  * @param $str (string) string from where to extract value 
  1236.  * @param $offset (int) point from where to read the data 
  1237.  * @return int 16 bit value 
  1238.  * @author Nicola Asuni 
  1239.  * @since 5.9.123 (2011-09-30) 
  1240.  * @public static 
  1241.  */ 
  1242. public static function _getFIXED($str, $offset) { 
  1243.     // mantissa 
  1244.     $m = self::_getFWORD($str, $offset); 
  1245.     // fraction 
  1246.     $f = self::_getUSHORT($str, ($offset + 2)); 
  1247.     $v = floatval(''.$m.'.'.$f.''); 
  1248.     return $v; 
  1249. } 
  1250.  
  1251. /** 
  1252.  * Get BYTE from string (8-bit unsigned integer). 
  1253.  * @param $str (string) String from where to extract value. 
  1254.  * @param $offset (int) Point from where to read the data. 
  1255.  * @return int 8 bit value 
  1256.  * @author Nicola Asuni 
  1257.  * @since 5.2.000 (2010-06-02)

  1259.  */ 
  1260. public static function _getBYTE($str, $offset) { 
  1261.     $v = unpack('Ci', substr($str, $offset, 1)); 
  1262.     return $v['i']; 
  1263. } 
  1264. /** 
  1265.  * Binary-safe and URL-safe file read. 
  1266.  * Reads up to length bytes from the file pointer referenced by handle. Reading stops as soon as one of the following conditions is met: length bytes have been read; EOF (end of file) is reached. 
  1267.  * @param $handle (resource) 
  1268.  * @param $length (int) 
  1269.  * @return Returns the read string or FALSE in case of error. 
  1270.  * @author Nicola Asuni 
  1271.  * @since 4.5.027 (2009-03-16) 
  1272.  * @public static 
  1273.  */ 
  1274. public static function rfread($handle, $length) { 
  1275.     $data = fread($handle, $length); 
  1276.     if ($data === false) { 
  1277.         return false; 
  1278.     } 
  1279.     $rest = ($length - strlen($data)); 
  1280.     if ($rest > 0) { 
  1281.         $data .= self::rfread($handle, $rest); 
  1282.     } 
  1283.     return $data; 
  1284. } 
  1285.  
  1286. /** 
  1287.  * Read a 4-byte (32 bit) integer from file. 
  1288.  * @param $f (string) file name. 
  1289.  * @return 4-byte integer 
  1290.  * @public static 
  1291.  */ 
  1292. public static function _freadint($f) { 
  1293.     $a = unpack('Ni', fread($f, 4)); 
  1294.     return $a['i']; 
  1295. } 
  1296.  
  1297. /** 
  1298.  * Returns a string containing random data to be used as a seed for encryption methods. 
  1299.  * @param $seed (string) starting seed value 
  1300.  * @return string containing random data 
  1301.  * @author Nicola Asuni 
  1302.  * @since 5.9.006 (2010-10-19) 
  1303.  * @public static 
  1304.  */ 
  1305. public static function getRandomSeed($seed='') { 
  1306.     $seed .= microtime(); 
  1307.     if (function_exists('openssl_random_pseudo_bytes') AND (strtoupper(substr(PHP_OS, 0, 3)) !== 'WIN')) { 
  1308.         // this is not used on windows systems because it is very slow for a know bug 
  1309.         $seed .= openssl_random_pseudo_bytes(512); 
  1310.     } else { 
  1311.         for ($i = 0; $i < 23; ++$i) { 
  1312.             $seed .= uniqid('', true); 
  1313.         } 
  1314.     } 
  1315.     $seed .= uniqid('', true); 
  1316.     $seed .= rand(); 
  1317.     $seed .= getmypid(); 
  1318.     $seed .= __FILE__; 
  1319.     if (isset($_SERVER['REMOTE_ADDR'])) { 
  1320.         $seed .= $_SERVER['REMOTE_ADDR']; 
  1321.     } 
  1322.     if (isset($_SERVER['HTTP_USER_AGENT'])) { 
  1323.         $seed .= $_SERVER['HTTP_USER_AGENT']; 
  1324.     } 
  1325.     if (isset($_SERVER['HTTP_ACCEPT'])) { 
  1326.         $seed .= $_SERVER['HTTP_ACCEPT']; 
  1327.     } 
  1328.     if (isset($_SERVER['HTTP_ACCEPT_ENCODING'])) { 
  1329.         $seed .= $_SERVER['HTTP_ACCEPT_ENCODING']; 
  1330.     } 
  1331.     if (isset($_SERVER['HTTP_ACCEPT_LANGUAGE'])) { 
  1332.         $seed .= $_SERVER['HTTP_ACCEPT_LANGUAGE']; 
  1333.     } 
  1334.     if (isset($_SERVER['HTTP_ACCEPT_CHARSET'])) { 
  1335.         $seed .= $_SERVER['HTTP_ACCEPT_CHARSET']; 
  1336.     } 
  1337.     $seed .= rand(); 
  1338.     $seed .= uniqid('', true); 
  1339.     $seed .= microtime(); 
  1340.     return $seed; 
  1341. } 
  1342.  
  1343. /** 
  1344.  * Encrypts a string using MD5 and returns it's value as a binary string. 
  1345.  * @param $str (string) input string 
  1346.  * @return String MD5 encrypted binary string 
  1347.  * @since 2.0.000 (2008-01-02) 
  1348.  * @public static 
  1349.  */ 
  1350. public static function _md5_16($str) { 
  1351.     return pack('H*', md5($str)); 
  1352. } 
  1353.  
  1354. /** 
  1355.  * Returns the input text exrypted using AES algorithm and the specified key. 
  1356.  * This method requires mcrypt. 
  1357.  * @param $key (string) encryption key 
  1358.  * @param $text (String) input text to be encrypted 
  1359.  * @return String encrypted text 
  1360.  * @author Nicola Asuni 
  1361.  * @since 5.0.005 (2010-05-11) 
  1362.  * @public static 
  1363.  */ 
  1364. public static function _AES($key, $text) { 
  1365.     // padding (RFC 2898, PKCS #5: Password-Based Cryptography Specification Version 2.0) 
  1366.     $padding = 16 - (strlen($text) % 16); 
  1367.     $text .= str_repeat(chr($padding), $padding); 
  1368.     $iv = mcrypt_create_iv(mcrypt_get_iv_size(MCRYPT_RIJNDAEL_128, MCRYPT_MODE_CBC), MCRYPT_RAND); 
  1369.     $text = mcrypt_encrypt(MCRYPT_RIJNDAEL_128, $key, $text, MCRYPT_MODE_CBC, $iv); 
  1370.     $text = $iv.$text; 
  1371.     return $text; 
  1372. } 
  1373.  
  1374. /** 
  1375.  * Returns the input text encrypted using RC4 algorithm and the specified key. 
  1376.  * RC4 is the standard encryption algorithm used in PDF format 
  1377.  * @param $key (string) Encryption key. 
  1378.  * @param $text (String) Input text to be encrypted. 
  1379.  * @param $last_enc_key (String) Reference to last RC4 key encrypted. 
  1380.  * @param $last_enc_key_c (String) Reference to last RC4 computed key. 
  1381.  * @return String encrypted text 
  1382.  * @since 2.0.000 (2008-01-02) 
  1383.  * @author Klemen Vodopivec, Nicola Asuni 
  1384.  * @public static 
  1385.  */ 
  1386. public static function _RC4($key, $text, &$last_enc_key, &$last_enc_key_c) { 
  1387.     if (function_exists('mcrypt_encrypt') AND ($out = @mcrypt_encrypt(MCRYPT_ARCFOUR, $key, $text, MCRYPT_MODE_STREAM, ''))) { 
  1388.         // try to use mcrypt function if exist 
  1389.         return $out; 
  1390.     } 
  1391.     if ($last_enc_key != $key) { 
  1392.         $k = str_repeat($key, ((256 / strlen($key)) + 1)); 
  1393.         $rc4 = range(0, 255); 
  1394.         $j = 0; 
  1395.         for ($i = 0; $i < 256; ++$i) { 
  1396.             $t = $rc4[$i]; 
  1397.             $j = ($j + $t + ord($k[$i])) % 256; 
  1398.             $rc4[$i] = $rc4[$j]; 
  1399.             $rc4[$j] = $t; 
  1400.         } 
  1401.         $last_enc_key = $key; 
  1402.         $last_enc_key_c = $rc4; 
  1403.     } else { 
  1404.         $rc4 = $last_enc_key_c; 
  1405.     } 
  1406.     $len = strlen($text); 
  1407.     $a = 0; 
  1408.     $b = 0; 
  1409.     $out = ''; 
  1410.     for ($i = 0; $i < $len; ++$i) { 
  1411.         $a = ($a + 1) % 256; 
  1412.         $t = $rc4[$a]; 
  1413.         $b = ($b + $t) % 256; 
  1414.         $rc4[$a] = $rc4[$b]; 
  1415.         $rc4[$b] = $t; 
  1416.         $k = $rc4[($rc4[$a] + $rc4[$b]) % 256]; 
  1417.         $out .= chr(ord($text[$i]) ^ $k); 
  1418.     } 
  1419.     return $out; 
  1420. } 
  1421.  
  1422. /** 
  1423.  * Return the premission code used on encryption (P value). 
  1424.  * @param $permissions (Array) the set of permissions (specify the ones you want to block). 
  1425.  * @param $mode (int) encryption strength: 0 = RC4 40 bit; 1 = RC4 128 bit; 2 = AES 128 bit; 3 = AES 256 bit. 
  1426.  * @since 5.0.005 (2010-05-12) 
  1427.  * @author Nicola Asuni 
  1428.  * @public static 
  1429.  */ 
  1430. public static function getUserPermissionCode($permissions, $mode=0) { 
  1431.     $options = array( 
  1432.         'owner' => 2, // bit 2 -- inverted logic: cleared by default 
  1433.         'print' => 4, // bit 3 
  1434.         'modify' => 8, // bit 4 
  1435.         'copy' => 16, // bit 5 
  1436.         'annot-forms' => 32, // bit 6 
  1437.         'fill-forms' => 256, // bit 9 
  1438.         'extract' => 512, // bit 10 
  1439.         'assemble' => 1024, // bit 11 
  1440.         'print-high' => 2048 // bit 12 
  1441.  ); 
  1442.     $protection = 2147422012; // 32 bit: (01111111 11111111 00001111 00111100) 
  1443.     foreach ($permissions as $permission) { 
  1444.         if (isset($options[$permission])) { 
  1445.             if (($mode > 0) OR ($options[$permission] <= 32)) { 
  1446.                 // set only valid permissions 
  1447.                 if ($options[$permission] == 2) { 
  1448.                     // the logic for bit 2 is inverted (cleared by default) 
  1449.                     $protection += $options[$permission]; 
  1450.                 } else { 
  1451.                     $protection -= $options[$permission]; 
  1452.                 } 
  1453.             } 
  1454.         } 
  1455.     } 
  1456.     return $protection; 
  1457. } 
  1458.  
  1459. /** 
  1460.  * Convert hexadecimal string to string 
  1461.  * @param $bs (string) byte-string to convert 
  1462.  * @return String 
  1463.  * @since 5.0.005 (2010-05-12) 
  1464.  * @author Nicola Asuni 
  1465.  * @public static 
  1466.  */ 
  1467. public static function convertHexStringToString($bs) { 
  1468.     $string = ''; // string to be returned 
  1469.     $bslength = strlen($bs); 
  1470.     if (($bslength % 2) != 0) { 
  1471.         // padding 
  1472.         $bs .= '0'; 
  1473.         ++$bslength; 
  1474.     } 
  1475.     for ($i = 0; $i < $bslength; $i += 2) { 
  1476.         $string .= chr(hexdec($bs[$i].$bs[($i + 1)])); 
  1477.     } 
  1478.     return $string; 
  1479. } 
  1480.  
  1481. /** 
  1482.  * Convert string to hexadecimal string (byte string) 
  1483.  * @param $s (string) string to convert 
  1484.  * @return byte string 
  1485.  * @since 5.0.010 (2010-05-17) 
  1486.  * @author Nicola Asuni 
  1487.  * @public static 
  1488.  */ 
  1489. public static function convertStringToHexString($s) { 
  1490.     $bs = ''; 
  1491.     $chars = preg_split('//', $s, -1, PREG_SPLIT_NO_EMPTY); 
  1492.     foreach ($chars as $c) { 
  1493.         $bs .= sprintf('%02s', dechex(ord($c))); 
  1494.     } 
  1495.     return $bs; 
  1496. } 
  1497.  
  1498. /** 
  1499.  * Convert encryption P value to a string of bytes, low-order byte first. 
  1500.  * @param $protection (string) 32bit encryption permission value (P value) 
  1501.  * @return String 
  1502.  * @since 5.0.005 (2010-05-12) 
  1503.  * @author Nicola Asuni 
  1504.  * @public static 
  1505.  */ 
  1506. public static function getEncPermissionsString($protection) { 
  1507.     $binprot = sprintf('%032b', $protection); 
  1508.     $str = chr(bindec(substr($binprot, 24, 8))); 
  1509.     $str .= chr(bindec(substr($binprot, 16, 8))); 
  1510.     $str .= chr(bindec(substr($binprot, 8, 8))); 
  1511.     $str .= chr(bindec(substr($binprot, 0, 8))); 
  1512.     return $str; 
  1513. } 
  1514.  
  1515. /** 
  1516.  * Encode a name object. 
  1517.  * @param $name (string) Name object to encode. 
  1518.  * @return (string) Encoded name object. 
  1519.  * @author Nicola Asuni 
  1520.  * @since 5.9.097 (2011-06-23) 
  1521.  * @public static 
  1522.  */ 
  1523. public static function encodeNameObject($name) { 
  1524.     $escname = ''; 
  1525.     $length = strlen($name); 
  1526.     for ($i = 0; $i < $length; ++$i) { 
  1527.         $chr = $name[$i]; 
  1528.         if (preg_match('/[0-9a-zA-Z#_=-]/', $chr) == 1) { 
  1529.             $escname .= $chr; 
  1530.         } else { 
  1531.             $escname .= sprintf('#%02X', ord($chr)); 
  1532.         } 
  1533.     } 
  1534.     return $escname; 
  1535. } 
  1536.  
  1537. /** 
  1538.  * Convert JavaScript form fields properties array to Annotation Properties array. 
  1539.  * @param $prop (array) javascript field properties. Possible values are described on official Javascript for Acrobat API reference. 
  1540.  * @param $spot_colors (array) Reference to spot colors array. 
  1541.  * @param $rtl (boolean) True if in Right-To-Left text direction mode, false otherwise. 
  1542.  * @return array of annotation properties 
  1543.  * @author Nicola Asuni 
  1544.  * @since 4.8.000 (2009-09-06) 
  1545.  * @public static 
  1546.  */ 
  1547. public static function getAnnotOptFromJSProp($prop, &$spot_colors, $rtl=false) { 
  1548.     if (isset($prop['aopt']) AND is_array($prop['aopt'])) { 
  1549.         // the annotation options area lready defined 
  1550.         return $prop['aopt']; 
  1551.     } 
  1552.     $opt = array(); // value to be returned 
  1553.     // alignment: Controls how the text is laid out within the text field. 
  1554.     if (isset($prop['alignment'])) { 
  1555.         switch ($prop['alignment']) { 
  1556.             case 'left': { 
  1557.                 $opt['q'] = 0; 
  1558.                 break; 
  1559.             } 
  1560.             case 'center': { 
  1561.                 $opt['q'] = 1; 
  1562.                 break; 
  1563.             } 
  1564.             case 'right': { 
  1565.                 $opt['q'] = 2; 
  1566.                 break; 
  1567.             } 
  1568.             default: { 
  1569.                 $opt['q'] = ($rtl)?2:0; 
  1570.                 break; 
  1571.             } 
  1572.         } 
  1573.     } 
  1574.     // lineWidth: Specifies the thickness of the border when stroking the perimeter of a field's rectangle. 
  1575.     if (isset($prop['lineWidth'])) { 
  1576.         $linewidth = intval($prop['lineWidth']); 
  1577.     } else { 
  1578.         $linewidth = 1; 
  1579.     } 
  1580.     // borderStyle: The border style for a field. 
  1581.     if (isset($prop['borderStyle'])) { 
  1582.         switch ($prop['borderStyle']) { 
  1583.             case 'border.d': 
  1584.             case 'dashed': { 
  1585.                 $opt['border'] = array(0, 0, $linewidth, array(3, 2)); 
  1586.                 $opt['bs'] = array('w'=>$linewidth, 's'=>'D', 'd'=>array(3, 2)); 
  1587.                 break; 
  1588.             } 
  1589.             case 'border.b': 
  1590.             case 'beveled': { 
  1591.                 $opt['border'] = array(0, 0, $linewidth); 
  1592.                 $opt['bs'] = array('w'=>$linewidth, 's'=>'B'); 
  1593.                 break; 
  1594.             } 
  1595.             case 'border.i': 
  1596.             case 'inset': { 
  1597.                 $opt['border'] = array(0, 0, $linewidth); 
  1598.                 $opt['bs'] = array('w'=>$linewidth, 's'=>'I'); 
  1599.                 break; 
  1600.             } 
  1601.             case 'border.u': 
  1602.             case 'underline': { 
  1603.                 $opt['border'] = array(0, 0, $linewidth); 
  1604.                 $opt['bs'] = array('w'=>$linewidth, 's'=>'U'); 
  1605.                 break; 
  1606.             } 
  1607.             case 'border.s': 
  1608.             case 'solid': { 
  1609.                 $opt['border'] = array(0, 0, $linewidth); 
  1610.                 $opt['bs'] = array('w'=>$linewidth, 's'=>'S'); 
  1611.                 break; 
  1612.             } 
  1613.             default: { 
  1614.                 break; 
  1615.             } 
  1616.         } 
  1617.     } 
  1618.     if (isset($prop['border']) AND is_array($prop['border'])) { 
  1619.         $opt['border'] = $prop['border']; 
  1620.     } 
  1621.     if (!isset($opt['mk'])) { 
  1622.         $opt['mk'] = array(); 
  1623.     } 
  1624.     if (!isset($opt['mk']['if'])) { 
  1625.         $opt['mk']['if'] = array(); 
  1626.     } 
  1627.     $opt['mk']['if']['a'] = array(0.5, 0.5); 
  1628.     // buttonAlignX: Controls how space is distributed from the left of the button face with respect to the icon. 
  1629.     if (isset($prop['buttonAlignX'])) { 
  1630.         $opt['mk']['if']['a'][0] = $prop['buttonAlignX']; 
  1631.     } 
  1632.     // buttonAlignY: Controls how unused space is distributed from the bottom of the button face with respect to the icon. 
  1633.     if (isset($prop['buttonAlignY'])) { 
  1634.         $opt['mk']['if']['a'][1] = $prop['buttonAlignY']; 
  1635.     } 
  1636.     // buttonFitBounds: If true, the extent to which the icon may be scaled is set to the bounds of the button field. 
  1637.     if (isset($prop['buttonFitBounds']) AND ($prop['buttonFitBounds'] == 'true')) { 
  1638.         $opt['mk']['if']['fb'] = true; 
  1639.     } 
  1640.     // buttonScaleHow: Controls how the icon is scaled (if necessary) to fit inside the button face. 
  1641.     if (isset($prop['buttonScaleHow'])) { 
  1642.         switch ($prop['buttonScaleHow']) { 
  1643.             case 'scaleHow.proportional': { 
  1644.                 $opt['mk']['if']['s'] = 'P'; 
  1645.                 break; 
  1646.             } 
  1647.             case 'scaleHow.anamorphic': { 
  1648.                 $opt['mk']['if']['s'] = 'A'; 
  1649.                 break; 
  1650.             } 
  1651.         } 
  1652.     } 
  1653.     // buttonScaleWhen: Controls when an icon is scaled to fit inside the button face. 
  1654.     if (isset($prop['buttonScaleWhen'])) { 
  1655.         switch ($prop['buttonScaleWhen']) { 
  1656.             case 'scaleWhen.always': { 
  1657.                 $opt['mk']['if']['sw'] = 'A'; 
  1658.                 break; 
  1659.             } 
  1660.             case 'scaleWhen.never': { 
  1661.                 $opt['mk']['if']['sw'] = 'N'; 
  1662.                 break; 
  1663.             } 
  1664.             case 'scaleWhen.tooBig': { 
  1665.                 $opt['mk']['if']['sw'] = 'B'; 
  1666.                 break; 
  1667.             } 
  1668.             case 'scaleWhen.tooSmall': { 
  1669.                 $opt['mk']['if']['sw'] = 'S'; 
  1670.                 break; 
  1671.             } 
  1672.         } 
  1673.     } 
  1674.     // buttonPosition: Controls how the text and the icon of the button are positioned with respect to each other within the button face. 
  1675.     if (isset($prop['buttonPosition'])) { 
  1676.         switch ($prop['buttonPosition']) { 
  1677.             case 0: 
  1678.             case 'position.textOnly': { 
  1679.                 $opt['mk']['tp'] = 0; 
  1680.                 break; 
  1681.             } 
  1682.             case 1: 
  1683.             case 'position.iconOnly': { 
  1684.                 $opt['mk']['tp'] = 1; 
  1685.                 break; 
  1686.             } 
  1687.             case 2: 
  1688.             case 'position.iconTextV': { 
  1689.                 $opt['mk']['tp'] = 2; 
  1690.                 break; 
  1691.             } 
  1692.             case 3: 
  1693.             case 'position.textIconV': { 
  1694.                 $opt['mk']['tp'] = 3; 
  1695.                 break; 
  1696.             } 
  1697.             case 4: 
  1698.             case 'position.iconTextH': { 
  1699.                 $opt['mk']['tp'] = 4; 
  1700.                 break; 
  1701.             } 
  1702.             case 5: 
  1703.             case 'position.textIconH': { 
  1704.                 $opt['mk']['tp'] = 5; 
  1705.                 break; 
  1706.             } 
  1707.             case 6: 
  1708.             case 'position.overlay': { 
  1709.                 $opt['mk']['tp'] = 6; 
  1710.                 break; 
  1711.             } 
  1712.         } 
  1713.     } 
  1714.     // fillColor: Specifies the background color for a field. 
  1715.     if (isset($prop['fillColor'])) { 
  1716.         if (is_array($prop['fillColor'])) { 
  1717.             $opt['mk']['bg'] = $prop['fillColor']; 
  1718.         } else { 
  1719.             $opt['mk']['bg'] = TCPDF_COLORS::convertHTMLColorToDec($prop['fillColor'], $spot_colors); 
  1720.         } 
  1721.     } 
  1722.     // strokeColor: Specifies the stroke color for a field that is used to stroke the rectangle of the field with a line as large as the line width. 
  1723.     if (isset($prop['strokeColor'])) { 
  1724.         if (is_array($prop['strokeColor'])) { 
  1725.             $opt['mk']['bc'] = $prop['strokeColor']; 
  1726.         } else { 
  1727.             $opt['mk']['bc'] = TCPDF_COLORS::convertHTMLColorToDec($prop['strokeColor'], $spot_colors); 
  1728.         } 
  1729.     } 
  1730.     // rotation: The rotation of a widget in counterclockwise increments. 
  1731.     if (isset($prop['rotation'])) { 
  1732.         $opt['mk']['r'] = $prop['rotation']; 
  1733.     } 
  1734.     // charLimit: Limits the number of characters that a user can type into a text field. 
  1735.     if (isset($prop['charLimit'])) { 
  1736.         $opt['maxlen'] = intval($prop['charLimit']); 
  1737.     } 
  1738.     if (!isset($ff)) { 
  1739.         $ff = 0; // default value 
  1740.     } 
  1741.     // readonly: The read-only characteristic of a field. If a field is read-only, the user can see the field but cannot change it. 
  1742.     if (isset($prop['readonly']) AND ($prop['readonly'] == 'true')) { 
  1743.         $ff += 1 << 0; 
  1744.     } 
  1745.     // required: Specifies whether a field requires a value. 
  1746.     if (isset($prop['required']) AND ($prop['required'] == 'true')) { 
  1747.         $ff += 1 << 1; 
  1748.     } 
  1749.     // multiline: Controls how text is wrapped within the field. 
  1750.     if (isset($prop['multiline']) AND ($prop['multiline'] == 'true')) { 
  1751.         $ff += 1 << 12; 
  1752.     } 
  1753.     // password: Specifies whether the field should display asterisks when data is entered in the field. 
  1754.     if (isset($prop['password']) AND ($prop['password'] == 'true')) { 
  1755.         $ff += 1 << 13; 
  1756.     } 
  1757.     // NoToggleToOff: If set, exactly one radio button shall be selected at all times; selecting the currently selected button has no effect. 
  1758.     if (isset($prop['NoToggleToOff']) AND ($prop['NoToggleToOff'] == 'true')) { 
  1759.         $ff += 1 << 14; 
  1760.     } 
  1761.     // Radio: If set, the field is a set of radio buttons. 
  1762.     if (isset($prop['Radio']) AND ($prop['Radio'] == 'true')) { 
  1763.         $ff += 1 << 15; 
  1764.     } 
  1765.     // Pushbutton: If set, the field is a pushbutton that does not retain a permanent value. 
  1766.     if (isset($prop['Pushbutton']) AND ($prop['Pushbutton'] == 'true')) { 
  1767.         $ff += 1 << 16; 
  1768.     } 
  1769.     // Combo: If set, the field is a combo box; if clear, the field is a list box. 
  1770.     if (isset($prop['Combo']) AND ($prop['Combo'] == 'true')) { 
  1771.         $ff += 1 << 17; 
  1772.     } 
  1773.     // editable: Controls whether a combo box is editable. 
  1774.     if (isset($prop['editable']) AND ($prop['editable'] == 'true')) { 
  1775.         $ff += 1 << 18; 
  1776.     } 
  1777.     // Sort: If set, the field's option items shall be sorted alphabetically. 
  1778.     if (isset($prop['Sort']) AND ($prop['Sort'] == 'true')) { 
  1779.         $ff += 1 << 19; 
  1780.     } 
  1781.     // fileSelect: If true, sets the file-select flag in the Options tab of the text field (Field is Used for File Selection). 
  1782.     if (isset($prop['fileSelect']) AND ($prop['fileSelect'] == 'true')) { 
  1783.         $ff += 1 << 20; 
  1784.     } 
  1785.     // multipleSelection: If true, indicates that a list box allows a multiple selection of items. 
  1786.     if (isset($prop['multipleSelection']) AND ($prop['multipleSelection'] == 'true')) { 
  1787.         $ff += 1 << 21; 
  1788.     } 
  1789.     // doNotSpellCheck: If true, spell checking is not performed on this editable text field. 
  1790.     if (isset($prop['doNotSpellCheck']) AND ($prop['doNotSpellCheck'] == 'true')) { 
  1791.         $ff += 1 << 22; 
  1792.     } 
  1793.     // doNotScroll: If true, the text field does not scroll and the user, therefore, is limited by the rectangular region designed for the field. 
  1794.     if (isset($prop['doNotScroll']) AND ($prop['doNotScroll'] == 'true')) { 
  1795.         $ff += 1 << 23; 
  1796.     } 
  1797.     // comb: If set to true, the field background is drawn as series of boxes (one for each character in the value of the field) and each character of the content is drawn within those boxes. The number of boxes drawn is determined from the charLimit property. It applies only to text fields. The setter will also raise if any of the following field properties are also set multiline, password, and fileSelect. A side-effect of setting this property is that the doNotScroll property is also set. 
  1798.     if (isset($prop['comb']) AND ($prop['comb'] == 'true')) { 
  1799.         $ff += 1 << 24; 
  1800.     } 
  1801.     // radiosInUnison: If false, even if a group of radio buttons have the same name and export value, they behave in a mutually exclusive fashion, like HTML radio buttons. 
  1802.     if (isset($prop['radiosInUnison']) AND ($prop['radiosInUnison'] == 'true')) { 
  1803.         $ff += 1 << 25; 
  1804.     } 
  1805.     // richText: If true, the field allows rich text formatting. 
  1806.     if (isset($prop['richText']) AND ($prop['richText'] == 'true')) { 
  1807.         $ff += 1 << 25; 
  1808.     } 
  1809.     // commitOnSelChange: Controls whether a field value is committed after a selection change. 
  1810.     if (isset($prop['commitOnSelChange']) AND ($prop['commitOnSelChange'] == 'true')) { 
  1811.         $ff += 1 << 26; 
  1812.     } 
  1813.     $opt['ff'] = $ff; 
  1814.     // defaultValue: The default value of a field - that is, the value that the field is set to when the form is reset. 
  1815.     if (isset($prop['defaultValue'])) { 
  1816.         $opt['dv'] = $prop['defaultValue']; 
  1817.     } 
  1818.     $f = 4; // default value for annotation flags 
  1819.     // readonly: The read-only characteristic of a field. If a field is read-only, the user can see the field but cannot change it. 
  1820.     if (isset($prop['readonly']) AND ($prop['readonly'] == 'true')) { 
  1821.         $f += 1 << 6; 
  1822.     } 
  1823.     // display: Controls whether the field is hidden or visible on screen and in print. 
  1824.     if (isset($prop['display'])) { 
  1825.         if ($prop['display'] == 'display.visible') { 
  1826.             // 
  1827.         } elseif ($prop['display'] == 'display.hidden') { 
  1828.             $f += 1 << 1; 
  1829.         } elseif ($prop['display'] == 'display.noPrint') { 
  1830.             $f -= 1 << 2; 
  1831.         } elseif ($prop['display'] == 'display.noView') { 
  1832.             $f += 1 << 5; 
  1833.         } 
  1834.     } 
  1835.     $opt['f'] = $f; 
  1836.     // currentValueIndices: Reads and writes single or multiple values of a list box or combo box. 
  1837.     if (isset($prop['currentValueIndices']) AND is_array($prop['currentValueIndices'])) { 
  1838.         $opt['i'] = $prop['currentValueIndices']; 
  1839.     } 
  1840.     // value: The value of the field data that the user has entered. 
  1841.     if (isset($prop['value'])) { 
  1842.         if (is_array($prop['value'])) { 
  1843.             $opt['opt'] = array(); 
  1844.             foreach ($prop['value'] AS $key => $optval) { 
  1845.                 // exportValues: An array of strings representing the export values for the field. 
  1846.                 if (isset($prop['exportValues'][$key])) { 
  1847.                     $opt['opt'][$key] = array($prop['exportValues'][$key], $prop['value'][$key]); 
  1848.                 } else { 
  1849.                     $opt['opt'][$key] = $prop['value'][$key]; 
  1850.                 } 
  1851.             } 
  1852.         } else { 
  1853.             $opt['v'] = $prop['value']; 
  1854.         } 
  1855.     } 
  1856.     // richValue: This property specifies the text contents and formatting of a rich text field. 
  1857.     if (isset($prop['richValue'])) { 
  1858.         $opt['rv'] = $prop['richValue']; 
  1859.     } 
  1860.     // submitName: If nonempty, used during form submission instead of name. Only applicable if submitting in HTML format (that is, URL-encoded). 
  1861.     if (isset($prop['submitName'])) { 
  1862.         $opt['tm'] = $prop['submitName']; 
  1863.     } 
  1864.     // name: Fully qualified field name. 
  1865.     if (isset($prop['name'])) { 
  1866.         $opt['t'] = $prop['name']; 
  1867.     } 
  1868.     // userName: The user name (short description string) of the field. 
  1869.     if (isset($prop['userName'])) { 
  1870.         $opt['tu'] = $prop['userName']; 
  1871.     } 
  1872.     // highlight: Defines how a button reacts when a user clicks it. 
  1873.     if (isset($prop['highlight'])) { 
  1874.         switch ($prop['highlight']) { 
  1875.             case 'none': 
  1876.             case 'highlight.n': { 
  1877.                 $opt['h'] = 'N'; 
  1878.                 break; 
  1879.             } 
  1880.             case 'invert': 
  1881.             case 'highlight.i': { 
  1882.                 $opt['h'] = 'i'; 
  1883.                 break; 
  1884.             } 
  1885.             case 'push': 
  1886.             case 'highlight.p': { 
  1887.                 $opt['h'] = 'P'; 
  1888.                 break; 
  1889.             } 
  1890.             case 'outline': 
  1891.             case 'highlight.o': { 
  1892.                 $opt['h'] = 'O'; 
  1893.                 break; 
  1894.             } 
  1895.         } 
  1896.     } 
  1897.     // Unsupported options: 
  1898.     // - calcOrderIndex: Changes the calculation order of fields in the document. 
  1899.     // - delay: Delays the redrawing of a field's appearance. 
  1900.     // - defaultStyle: This property defines the default style attributes for the form field. 
  1901.     // - style: Allows the user to set the glyph style of a check box or radio button. 
  1902.     // - textColor, textFont, textSize 
  1903.     return $opt; 
  1904. }

  1906. /** 
  1907.  * Format the page numbers. 
  1908.  * This method can be overriden for custom formats. 
  1909.  * @param $num (int) page number 
  1910.  * @since 4.2.005 (2008-11-06) 
  1911.  * @public static 
  1912.  */ 
  1913. public static function formatPageNumber($num) { 
  1914.     return number_format((float)$num, 0, '', '.'); 
  1915. } 
  1916.  
  1917. /** 
  1918.  * Format the page numbers on the Table Of Content. 
  1919.  * This method can be overriden for custom formats. 
  1920.  * @param $num (int) page number 
  1921.  * @since 4.5.001 (2009-01-04) 
  1922.  * @see addTOC(), addHTMLTOC() 
  1923.  * @public static 
  1924.  */ 
  1925. public static function formatTOCPageNumber($num) { 
  1926.     return number_format((float)$num, 0, '', '.'); 
  1927. } 
  1928.  
  1929. /** 
  1930.  * Extracts the CSS properties from a CSS string. 
  1931.  * @param $cssdata (string) string containing CSS definitions. 
  1932.  * @return An array where the keys are the CSS selectors and the values are the CSS properties. 
  1933.  * @author Nicola Asuni 
  1934.  * @since 5.1.000 (2010-05-25) 
  1935.  * @public static 
  1936.  */ 
  1937. public static function extractCSSproperties($cssdata) { 
  1938.     if (empty($cssdata)) { 
  1939.         return array(); 
  1940.     } 
  1941.     // remove comments 
  1942.     $cssdata = preg_replace('/\/\*[^\*]*\*\//', '', $cssdata); 
  1943.     // remove newlines and multiple spaces 
  1944.     $cssdata = preg_replace('/[\s]+/', ' ', $cssdata); 
  1945.     // remove some spaces 
  1946.     $cssdata = preg_replace('/[\s]*([;:\{\}]{1})[\s]*/', '\\1', $cssdata); 
  1947.     // remove empty blocks 
  1948.     $cssdata = preg_replace('/([^\}\{]+)\{\}/', '', $cssdata); 
  1949.     // replace media type parenthesis 
  1950.     $cssdata = preg_replace('/@media[\s]+([^\{]*)\{/i', '@media \\1', $cssdata); 
  1951.     $cssdata = preg_replace('/\}\}/si', '}', $cssdata); 
  1952.     // trim string 
  1953.     $cssdata = trim($cssdata); 
  1954.     // find media blocks (all, braille, embossed, handheld, print, projection, screen, speech, tty, tv) 
  1955.     $cssblocks = array(); 
  1956.     $matches = array(); 
  1957.     if (preg_match_all('/@media[\s]+([^\]*)([^]*)/i', $cssdata, $matches) > 0) { 
  1958.         foreach ($matches[1] as $key => $type) { 
  1959.             $cssblocks[$type] = $matches[2][$key]; 
  1960.         } 
  1961.         // remove media blocks 
  1962.         $cssdata = preg_replace('/@media[\s]+([^\]*)([^]*)/i', '', $cssdata); 
  1963.     } 
  1964.     // keep 'all' and 'print' media, other media types are discarded 
  1965.     if (isset($cssblocks['all']) AND !empty($cssblocks['all'])) { 
  1966.         $cssdata .= $cssblocks['all']; 
  1967.     } 
  1968.     if (isset($cssblocks['print']) AND !empty($cssblocks['print'])) { 
  1969.         $cssdata .= $cssblocks['print']; 
  1970.     } 
  1971.     // reset css blocks array 
  1972.     $cssblocks = array(); 
  1973.     $matches = array(); 
  1974.     // explode css data string into array 
  1975.     if (substr($cssdata, -1) == '}') { 
  1976.         // remove last parethesis 
  1977.         $cssdata = substr($cssdata, 0, -1); 
  1978.     } 
  1979.     $matches = explode('}', $cssdata); 
  1980.     foreach ($matches as $key => $block) { 
  1981.         // index 0 contains the CSS selector, index 1 contains CSS properties 
  1982.         $cssblocks[$key] = explode('{', $block); 
  1983.         if (!isset($cssblocks[$key][1])) { 
  1984.             // remove empty definitions 
  1985.             unset($cssblocks[$key]); 
  1986.         } 
  1987.     } 
  1988.     // split groups of selectors (comma-separated list of selectors) 
  1989.     foreach ($cssblocks as $key => $block) { 
  1990.         if (strpos($block[0], ', ') > 0) { 
  1991.             $selectors = explode(', ', $block[0]); 
  1992.             foreach ($selectors as $sel) { 
  1993.                 $cssblocks[] = array(0 => trim($sel), 1 => $block[1]); 
  1994.             } 
  1995.             unset($cssblocks[$key]); 
  1996.         } 
  1997.     } 
  1998.     // covert array to selector => properties 
  1999.     $cssdata = array(); 
  2000.     foreach ($cssblocks as $block) { 
  2001.         $selector = $block[0]; 
  2002.         // calculate selector's specificity 
  2003.         $matches = array(); 
  2004.         $a = 0; // the declaration is not from is a 'style' attribute 
  2005.         $b = intval(preg_match_all('/[\#]/', $selector, $matches)); // number of ID attributes 
  2006.         $c = intval(preg_match_all('/[\[\.]/', $selector, $matches)); // number of other attributes 
  2007.         $c += intval(preg_match_all('/[\:]link|visited|hover|active|focus|target|lang|enabled|disabled|checked|indeterminate|root|nth|first|last|only|empty|contains|not/i', $selector, $matches)); // number of pseudo-classes 
  2008.         $d = intval(preg_match_all('/[\>\+\~\s]{1}[a-zA-Z0-9]+/', ' '.$selector, $matches)); // number of element names 
  2009.         $d += intval(preg_match_all('/[\:][\:]/', $selector, $matches)); // number of pseudo-elements 
  2010.         $specificity = $a.$b.$c.$d; 
  2011.         // add specificity to the beginning of the selector 
  2012.         $cssdata[$specificity.' '.$selector] = $block[1]; 
  2013.     } 
  2014.     // sort selectors alphabetically to account for specificity 
  2015.     ksort($cssdata, SORT_STRING); 
  2016.     // return array 
  2017.     return $cssdata; 
  2018. } 
  2019.  
  2020. /** 
  2021.  * Cleanup HTML code (requires HTML Tidy library). 
  2022.  * @param $html (string) htmlcode to fix 
  2023.  * @param $default_css (string) CSS commands to add 
  2024.  * @param $tagvs (array) parameters for setHtmlVSpace method 
  2025.  * @param $tidy_options (array) options for tidy_parse_string function 
  2026.  * @param $tagvspaces (array) Array of vertical spaces for tags. 
  2027.  * @return string XHTML code cleaned up 
  2028.  * @author Nicola Asuni 
  2029.  * @since 5.9.017 (2010-11-16) 
  2030.  * @see setHtmlVSpace() 
  2031.  * @public static 
  2032.  */ 
  2033. public static function fixHTMLCode($html, $default_css='', $tagvs='', $tidy_options='', &$tagvspaces) { 
  2034.     // configure parameters for HTML Tidy 
  2035.     if ($tidy_options === '') { 
  2036.         $tidy_options = array ( 
  2037.             'clean' => 1,  
  2038.             'drop-empty-paras' => 0,  
  2039.             'drop-proprietary-attributes' => 1,  
  2040.             'fix-backslash' => 1,  
  2041.             'hide-comments' => 1,  
  2042.             'join-styles' => 1,  
  2043.             'lower-literals' => 1,  
  2044.             'merge-divs' => 1,  
  2045.             'merge-spans' => 1,  
  2046.             'output-xhtml' => 1,  
  2047.             'word-2000' => 1,  
  2048.             'wrap' => 0,  
  2049.             'output-bom' => 0,  
  2050.             //'char-encoding' => 'utf8',  
  2051.             //'input-encoding' => 'utf8',  
  2052.             //'output-encoding' => 'utf8' 
  2053.  ); 
  2054.     } 
  2055.     // clean up the HTML code 
  2056.     $tidy = tidy_parse_string($html, $tidy_options); 
  2057.     // fix the HTML 
  2058.     $tidy->cleanRepair(); 
  2059.     // get the CSS part 
  2060.     $tidy_head = tidy_get_head($tidy); 
  2061.     $css = $tidy_head->value; 
  2062.     $css = preg_replace('/<style([^>]+)>/ims', '<style>', $css); 
  2063.     $css = preg_replace('/<\/style>(.*)<style>/ims', "\n", $css); 
  2064.     $css = str_replace('/*<![CDATA[*/', '', $css); 
  2065.     $css = str_replace('/*]]>*/', '', $css); 
  2066.     preg_match('/<style>(.*)<\/style>/ims', $css, $matches); 
  2067.     if (isset($matches[1])) { 
  2068.         $css = strtolower($matches[1]); 
  2069.     } else { 
  2070.         $css = ''; 
  2071.     } 
  2072.     // include default css 
  2073.     $css = '<style>'.$default_css.$css.'</style>'; 
  2074.     // get the body part 
  2075.     $tidy_body = tidy_get_body($tidy); 
  2076.     $html = $tidy_body->value; 
  2077.     // fix some self-closing tags 
  2078.     $html = str_replace('<br>', '<br />', $html); 
  2079.     // remove some empty tag blocks 
  2080.     $html = preg_replace('/<div([^\>]*)><\/div>/', '', $html); 
  2081.     $html = preg_replace('/<p([^\>]*)><\/p>/', '', $html); 
  2082.     if ($tagvs !== '') { 
  2083.         // set vertical space for some XHTML tags 
  2084.         $tagvspaces = $tagvs; 
  2085.     } 
  2086.     // return the cleaned XHTML code + CSS 
  2087.     return $css.$html; 
  2088. } 
  2089.  
  2090. /** 
  2091.  * Returns true if the CSS selector is valid for the selected HTML tag 
  2092.  * @param $dom (array) array of HTML tags and properties 
  2093.  * @param $key (int) key of the current HTML tag 
  2094.  * @param $selector (string) CSS selector string 
  2095.  * @return true if the selector is valid, false otherwise 
  2096.  * @since 5.1.000 (2010-05-25) 
  2097.  * @public static 
  2098.  */ 
  2099. public static function isValidCSSSelectorForTag($dom, $key, $selector) { 
  2100.     $valid = false; // value to be returned 
  2101.     $tag = $dom[$key]['value']; 
  2102.     $class = array(); 
  2103.     if (isset($dom[$key]['attribute']['class']) AND !empty($dom[$key]['attribute']['class'])) { 
  2104.         $class = explode(' ', strtolower($dom[$key]['attribute']['class'])); 
  2105.     } 
  2106.     $id = ''; 
  2107.     if (isset($dom[$key]['attribute']['id']) AND !empty($dom[$key]['attribute']['id'])) { 
  2108.         $id = strtolower($dom[$key]['attribute']['id']); 
  2109.     } 
  2110.     $selector = preg_replace('/([\>\+\~\s]{1})([\.]{1})([^\>\+\~\s]*)/si', '\\1*.\\3', $selector); 
  2111.     $matches = array(); 
  2112.     if (preg_match_all('/([\>\+\~\s]{1})([a-zA-Z0-9\*]+)([^\>\+\~\s]*)/si', $selector, $matches, PREG_PATTERN_ORDER | PREG_OFFSET_CAPTURE) > 0) { 
  2113.         $parentop = array_pop($matches[1]); 
  2114.         $operator = $parentop[0]; 
  2115.         $offset = $parentop[1]; 
  2116.         $lasttag = array_pop($matches[2]); 
  2117.         $lasttag = strtolower(trim($lasttag[0])); 
  2118.         if (($lasttag == '*') OR ($lasttag == $tag)) { 
  2119.             // the last element on selector is our tag or 'any tag' 
  2120.             $attrib = array_pop($matches[3]); 
  2121.             $attrib = strtolower(trim($attrib[0])); 
  2122.             if (!empty($attrib)) { 
  2123.                 // check if matches class, id, attribute, pseudo-class or pseudo-element 
  2124.                 switch ($attrib[0]) { 
  2125.                     case '.': { // class 
  2126.                         if (in_array(substr($attrib, 1), $class)) { 
  2127.                             $valid = true; 
  2128.                         } 
  2129.                         break; 
  2130.                     } 
  2131.                     case '#': { // ID 
  2132.                         if (substr($attrib, 1) == $id) { 
  2133.                             $valid = true; 
  2134.                         } 
  2135.                         break; 
  2136.                     } 
  2137.                     case '[': { // attribute 
  2138.                         $attrmatch = array(); 
  2139.                         if (preg_match('/\[([a-zA-Z0-9]*)[\s]*([\~\^\$\*\|\=]*)[\s]*["]?([^"\]]*)["]?\]/i', $attrib, $attrmatch) > 0) { 
  2140.                             $att = strtolower($attrmatch[1]); 
  2141.                             $val = $attrmatch[3]; 
  2142.                             if (isset($dom[$key]['attribute'][$att])) { 
  2143.                                 switch ($attrmatch[2]) { 
  2144.                                     case '=': { 
  2145.                                         if ($dom[$key]['attribute'][$att] == $val) { 
  2146.                                             $valid = true; 
  2147.                                         } 
  2148.                                         break; 
  2149.                                     } 
  2150.                                     case '~=': { 
  2151.                                         if (in_array($val, explode(' ', $dom[$key]['attribute'][$att]))) { 
  2152.                                             $valid = true; 
  2153.                                         } 
  2154.                                         break; 
  2155.                                     } 
  2156.                                     case '^=': { 
  2157.                                         if ($val == substr($dom[$key]['attribute'][$att], 0, strlen($val))) { 
  2158.                                             $valid = true; 
  2159.                                         } 
  2160.                                         break; 
  2161.                                     } 
  2162.                                     case '$=': { 
  2163.                                         if ($val == substr($dom[$key]['attribute'][$att], -strlen($val))) { 
  2164.                                             $valid = true; 
  2165.                                         } 
  2166.                                         break; 
  2167.                                     } 
  2168.                                     case '*=': { 
  2169.                                         if (strpos($dom[$key]['attribute'][$att], $val) !== false) { 
  2170.                                             $valid = true; 
  2171.                                         } 
  2172.                                         break; 
  2173.                                     } 
  2174.                                     case '|=': { 
  2175.                                         if ($dom[$key]['attribute'][$att] == $val) { 
  2176.                                             $valid = true; 
  2177.                                         } elseif (preg_match('/'.$val.'[\-]{1}/i', $dom[$key]['attribute'][$att]) > 0) { 
  2178.                                             $valid = true; 
  2179.                                         } 
  2180.                                         break; 
  2181.                                     } 
  2182.                                     default: { 
  2183.                                         $valid = true; 
  2184.                                     } 
  2185.                                 } 
  2186.                             } 
  2187.                         } 
  2188.                         break; 
  2189.                     } 
  2190.                     case ':': { // pseudo-class or pseudo-element 
  2191.                         if ($attrib[1] == ':') { // pseudo-element 
  2192.                             // pseudo-elements are not supported! 
  2193.                             // (::first-line, ::first-letter, ::before, ::after) 
  2194.                         } else { // pseudo-class 
  2195.                             // pseudo-classes are not supported! 
  2196.                             // (:root, :nth-child(n), :nth-last-child(n), :nth-of-type(n), :nth-last-of-type(n), :first-child, :last-child, :first-of-type, :last-of-type, :only-child, :only-of-type, :empty, :link, :visited, :active, :hover, :focus, :target, :lang(fr), :enabled, :disabled, :checked) 
  2197.                         } 
  2198.                         break; 
  2199.                     } 
  2200.                 } // end of switch 
  2201.             } else { 
  2202.                 $valid = true; 
  2203.             } 
  2204.             if ($valid AND ($offset > 0)) { 
  2205.                 $valid = false; 
  2206.                 // check remaining selector part 
  2207.                 $selector = substr($selector, 0, $offset); 
  2208.                 switch ($operator) { 
  2209.                     case ' ': { // descendant of an element 
  2210.                         while ($dom[$key]['parent'] > 0) { 
  2211.                             if (self::isValidCSSSelectorForTag($dom, $dom[$key]['parent'], $selector)) { 
  2212.                                 $valid = true; 
  2213.                                 break; 
  2214.                             } else { 
  2215.                                 $key = $dom[$key]['parent']; 
  2216.                             } 
  2217.                         } 
  2218.                         break; 
  2219.                     } 
  2220.                     case '>': { // child of an element 
  2221.                         $valid = self::isValidCSSSelectorForTag($dom, $dom[$key]['parent'], $selector); 
  2222.                         break; 
  2223.                     } 
  2224.                     case '+': { // immediately preceded by an element 
  2225.                         for ($i = ($key - 1); $i > $dom[$key]['parent']; --$i) { 
  2226.                             if ($dom[$i]['tag'] AND $dom[$i]['opening']) { 
  2227.                                 $valid = self::isValidCSSSelectorForTag($dom, $i, $selector); 
  2228.                                 break; 
  2229.                             } 
  2230.                         } 
  2231.                         break; 
  2232.                     } 
  2233.                     case '~': { // preceded by an element 
  2234.                         for ($i = ($key - 1); $i > $dom[$key]['parent']; --$i) { 
  2235.                             if ($dom[$i]['tag'] AND $dom[$i]['opening']) { 
  2236.                                 if (self::isValidCSSSelectorForTag($dom, $i, $selector)) { 
  2237.                                     break; 
  2238.                                 } 
  2239.                             } 
  2240.                         } 
  2241.                         break; 
  2242.                     } 
  2243.                 } 
  2244.             } 
  2245.         } 
  2246.     } 
  2247.     return $valid; 
  2248. } 
  2249.  
  2250. /** 
  2251.  * Returns the styles array that apply for the selected HTML tag. 
  2252.  * @param $dom (array) array of HTML tags and properties 
  2253.  * @param $key (int) key of the current HTML tag 
  2254.  * @param $css (array) array of CSS properties 
  2255.  * @return array containing CSS properties 
  2256.  * @since 5.1.000 (2010-05-25) 
  2257.  * @public static 
  2258.  */ 
  2259. public static function getCSSdataArray($dom, $key, $css) { 
  2260.     $cssarray = array(); // style to be returned 
  2261.     // get parent CSS selectors 
  2262.     $selectors = array(); 
  2263.     if (isset($dom[($dom[$key]['parent'])]['csssel'])) { 
  2264.         $selectors = $dom[($dom[$key]['parent'])]['csssel']; 
  2265.     } 
  2266.     // get all styles that apply 
  2267.     foreach($css as $selector => $style) { 
  2268.         $pos = strpos($selector, ' '); 
  2269.         // get specificity 
  2270.         $specificity = substr($selector, 0, $pos); 
  2271.         // remove specificity 
  2272.         $selector = substr($selector, $pos); 
  2273.         // check if this selector apply to current tag 
  2274.         if (self::isValidCSSSelectorForTag($dom, $key, $selector)) { 
  2275.             if (!in_array($selector, $selectors)) { 
  2276.                 // add style if not already added on parent selector 
  2277.                 $cssarray[] = array('k' => $selector, 's' => $specificity, 'c' => $style); 
  2278.                 $selectors[] = $selector; 
  2279.             } 
  2280.         } 
  2281.     } 
  2282.     if (isset($dom[$key]['attribute']['style'])) { 
  2283.         // attach inline style (latest properties have high priority) 
  2284.         $cssarray[] = array('k' => '', 's' => '1000', 'c' => $dom[$key]['attribute']['style']); 
  2285.     } 
  2286.     // order the css array to account for specificity 
  2287.     $cssordered = array(); 
  2288.     foreach ($cssarray as $key => $val) { 
  2289.         $skey = sprintf('%04d', $key); 
  2290.         $cssordered[$val['s'].'_'.$skey] = $val; 
  2291.     } 
  2292.     // sort selectors alphabetically to account for specificity 
  2293.     ksort($cssordered, SORT_STRING); 
  2294.     return array($selectors, $cssordered); 
  2295. } 
  2296.  
  2297. /** 
  2298.  * Compact CSS data array into single string. 
  2299.  * @param $css (array) array of CSS properties 
  2300.  * @return string containing merged CSS properties 
  2301.  * @since 5.9.070 (2011-04-19) 
  2302.  * @public static 
  2303.  */ 
  2304. public static function getTagStyleFromCSSarray($css) { 
  2305.     $tagstyle = ''; // value to be returned 
  2306.     foreach ($css as $style) { 
  2307.         // split single css commands 
  2308.         $csscmds = explode(';', $style['c']); 
  2309.         foreach ($csscmds as $cmd) { 
  2310.             if (!empty($cmd)) { 
  2311.                 $pos = strpos($cmd, ':'); 
  2312.                 if ($pos !== false) { 
  2313.                     $cmd = substr($cmd, 0, ($pos + 1)); 
  2314.                     if (strpos($tagstyle, $cmd) !== false) { 
  2315.                         // remove duplicate commands (last commands have high priority) 
  2316.                         $tagstyle = preg_replace('/'.$cmd.'[^;]+/i', '', $tagstyle); 
  2317.                     } 
  2318.                 } 
  2319.             } 
  2320.         } 
  2321.         $tagstyle .= ';'.$style['c']; 
  2322.     } 
  2323.     // remove multiple semicolons 
  2324.     $tagstyle = preg_replace('/[;]+/', ';', $tagstyle); 
  2325.     return $tagstyle; 
  2326. } 
  2327.  
  2328. /** 
  2329.  * Returns the Roman representation of an integer number 
  2330.  * @param $number (int) number to convert 
  2331.  * @return string roman representation of the specified number 
  2332.  * @since 4.3.004 (2008-12-10) 
  2333.  * @public static 
  2334.  */ 
  2335. public static function intToRoman($number) { 
  2336.     $roman = ''; 
  2337.     while ($number >= 1000) { 
  2338.         $roman .= 'M'; 
  2339.         $number -= 1000; 
  2340.     } 
  2341.     while ($number >= 900) { 
  2342.         $roman .= 'CM'; 
  2343.         $number -= 900; 
  2344.     } 
  2345.     while ($number >= 500) { 
  2346.         $roman .= 'D'; 
  2347.         $number -= 500; 
  2348.     } 
  2349.     while ($number >= 400) { 
  2350.         $roman .= 'CD'; 
  2351.         $number -= 400; 
  2352.     } 
  2353.     while ($number >= 100) { 
  2354.         $roman .= 'C'; 
  2355.         $number -= 100; 
  2356.     } 
  2357.     while ($number >= 90) { 
  2358.         $roman .= 'XC'; 
  2359.         $number -= 90; 
  2360.     } 
  2361.     while ($number >= 50) { 
  2362.         $roman .= 'L'; 
  2363.         $number -= 50; 
  2364.     } 
  2365.     while ($number >= 40) { 
  2366.         $roman .= 'XL'; 
  2367.         $number -= 40; 
  2368.     } 
  2369.     while ($number >= 10) { 
  2370.         $roman .= 'X'; 
  2371.         $number -= 10; 
  2372.     } 
  2373.     while ($number >= 9) { 
  2374.         $roman .= 'IX'; 
  2375.         $number -= 9; 
  2376.     } 
  2377.     while ($number >= 5) { 
  2378.         $roman .= 'V'; 
  2379.         $number -= 5; 
  2380.     } 
  2381.     while ($number >= 4) { 
  2382.         $roman .= 'IV'; 
  2383.         $number -= 4; 
  2384.     } 
  2385.     while ($number >= 1) { 
  2386.         $roman .= 'I'; 
  2387.         --$number; 
  2388.     } 
  2389.     return $roman; 
  2390. } 
  2391.  
  2392. /** 
  2393.  * Find position of last occurrence of a substring in a string 
  2394.  * @param $haystack (string) The string to search in. 
  2395.  * @param $needle (string) substring to search. 
  2396.  * @param $offset (int) May be specified to begin searching an arbitrary number of characters into the string. 
  2397.  * @return Returns the position where the needle exists. Returns FALSE if the needle was not found. 
  2398.  * @since 4.8.038 (2010-03-13) 
  2399.  * @public static 
  2400.  */ 
  2401. public static function revstrpos($haystack, $needle, $offset = 0) { 
  2402.     $length = strlen($haystack); 
  2403.     $offset = ($offset > 0)?($length - $offset):abs($offset); 
  2404.     $pos = strpos(strrev($haystack), strrev($needle), $offset); 
  2405.     return ($pos === false)?false:($length - $pos - strlen($needle)); 
  2406. }

  2413.  * @public static 
  2414.  */ 
  2415. public static function serializeTCPDFtagParameters($pararray) { 
  2416.     return urlencode(serialize($pararray)); 
  2417. }
